FUNDING\n\nDesign for High-Speed\n\nDavis\n\nContractor Report\n\nSUBTITLE\n\nGuidance and Control\n\nof Ibis\n\nNUMBERS\n\nNAS1-19703\nTask 7\n5 38-04-13-02\n\nRollout and Turnoff (ROTO)\n\n6, _\xc2\xa2rrHows)\nS. H. Goldthorpe, R. D. Dangamn, J. P. Dwyer, L. S. McBee,\nR. M. Norman, J. H. Shannon, L. G. Summers\n7.\n\nPERFORMING\n\nORGANIZATION\n\nNAME(S)\n\nAND\n\nADDRESS(ES)\n\n8.\n\nMcDonnell Douglas Corporation\nMcDonnell Douglas Aerospace\nTransport Aircraft\n2401 E. SPONSORING\n\nI MONITORING\n\nAGENCY\n\nNAME(S)\n\nAND\n\nADDRESS(ES)\n\n10.\n\n11.\n\nSUPPLEMENTARY\n\nDISTRIBUTION\n\n/ MONITORING\n\nREPORT\n\nNUMBER\n\nNASA CR-201602\n\nNOTES\n\nLangley Technical Monitor:\nFinal Report\n12a.\n\nSPONSORING\nAGENCY\n\nNational Aeronautics and Space Administration\nLangley Research Center\nHampton, VA 23681-0001\n\nI AVAILAJ_LITY\n\nRichard M. Hueschen\n\nSTATEMENT\n\n12b.\n\nDISTRIBUTION\n\nCODE\n\nUnclassified - Unlimited\nSubject Category 08\n\n13.\n\nABSTI_CT\n\nl\'_udm_m\n\n200\n\nwords)\n\nA ROTO architecture, braking and steering control law and display designs for a research high speed Roliout and Turnoff (ROTO)\nsystem applicable to transportclass aircraft_ described herein. Minimum surface friction and FMS database requirements are also\ndocumented. The control law designs were developed with the aid of a non-real time simulation program incorporating airframesad gear\ndynamics as well as steering and braking guidance algorithms. An attainable objective of this ROTO system, as seen from the results of\nthis study, is to assure that the studied aircraftcan land with runway occupancy times less then 53 seconds. Runway occupancy time is\nmeasured f_m the time the aircraftcrosses the runway threshold until its wing tip clears the nea_ side of the runway. Turnoff ground\nspeeds of 70 knots onto 30 degree exits are allowed with dry and wet surface conditions. Simulation time history and statistical data are\ndocumented herein. Parameterswhich were treatedas variables in the simulation study include aircrafttouchdown weight/speed/location,\naixcraftCG, runway friction, sensor noise and winds. After furtherdesign and development of the ROTO control systembeyond the\nsystem developed in reference 1, aft CG ME)-11 aircraftno longer requireauto-asymmetric braking (steering) and fly-by-wire nose gear\nsteering.
